# Ecosystem Controlled Execution 1000 Plan — Draft Until Validated

## Executive Summary

This document is an execution register, not an execution command. It moves the ecosystem from cleanup mode into controlled execution, proof, and commercial output while keeping SourceA, Noetfield, TrustField, and NOOS independently owned.

Every item is written so an agent can either execute it in a future authorized lane or reject it with a specific blocker. No item should be executed merely because it appears here. Runtime receipt churn remains runtime evidence unless explicitly snapshotted by policy.

Hard operating law: one repo, one lane, one commit; clean tree before and after every lane; no parallel agents in the same repo; no generated/evidence/backlog loose dirty files; use contracts, exports, manifests, and public APIs instead of internal cross-repo scripts; reserve high intelligence for decisions and reviews, not bulk scanning.

## Validation Criteria

- Exactly 1000 unique `PLAN-0001` through `PLAN-1000` IDs.
- No duplicate PLAN IDs except references in `Best First 25 To Execute`.
- Every PLAN row contains `Repo/scope`, `Priority`, `Lane`, `Artifact/system`, `Action`, `Success check`, and `Blocker risk`.
- No row uses a generic action unless it names a concrete artifact/system and outcome.
- Section counts must be A=50, B=75, C=125, D=150, E=100, F=125, G=100, H=75, I=100, J=50, K=50.
- This file remains `draft_until_validated` until a reviewer accepts these criteria and explicitly promotes it.

## B. Repo Policy Hardening — 75 Items

Turn cleanup lessons into machine-readable repo rules and clean-tree behavior.

- PLAN-0051 | Repo/scope: SourceA repo policy | Priority: P0 | Lane: Repo-Policy-Hardening:.cursor-rules-` | Artifact/system: `.cursor/rules/` lane rule | Action: Add a Cursor rule that rejects cross-repo edits for this lane. | Success check: repo-policy validator passes on the current tree. | Blocker risk: rule is too weak and permits cross-repo contamination.
- PLAN-0052 | Repo/scope: Noetfield website repo policy | Priority: P0 | Lane: Repo-Policy-Hardening:scripts-check_*policy*.p | Artifact/system: `scripts/check_*policy*.py` validator | Action: Define which evidence paths are ignored, snapshotted, restored, or committed. | Success check: evidence policy names at least restore and snapshot outcomes. | Blocker risk: classification language is ambiguous.
- PLAN-0053 | Repo/scope: TrustField repo policy | Priority: P1 | Lane: Repo-Policy-Hardening:generated-evidence | Artifact/system: generated/evidence path policy | Action: Define stable summary receipts separately from raw JSON/JSONL churn. | Success check: README line points to the exact validator command. | Blocker risk: validator depends on unavailable local state.
- PLAN-0054 | Repo/scope: NOOS repo policy | Priority: P1 | Lane: Repo-Policy-Hardening:dirty-file | Artifact/system: dirty-file classification table | Action: Add a machine-readable check that fails on forbidden product vocabulary or foreign paths. | Success check: Cursor rule contains explicit allowed and denied path patterns. | Blocker risk: runtime receipts remain volatile in git status.
- PLAN-0055 | Repo/scope: shared Cursor policy guidance | Priority: P2 | Lane: Repo-Policy-Hardening:runtime | Artifact/system: runtime receipt snapshot rule | Action: Create a table of dirty-file classes and allowed dispositions. | Success check: clean-tree guard reports generated churn separately from source docs. | Blocker risk: evidence policy hides needed audit artifacts.
